;;; Check whether atom is space comparing its type with type of the &self atom
  (: is-space 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-space $atom) 
    (let* 
      ( ($type (get-type $atom)) ($space (get-type &self))) 
      (== $type $space)))
  !(assertEqual 
    (is-space &self) True)
